Super Early Bird Tickets are our cheapest and are each year available right after the festival ends. Once these have sold out, the prices rise a little to the next level which is regular Early Bird Tickets. Once these have sold out we go to Tier 1. This method rewards those who buy early and helps to balance supply and demand for our tickets. \n \nTERMS AND CONDITIONS \nTickets are non-refundable except if the festival is cancelled, Standon Calling has been negligent or acted in breach of contract.
